val csvFeederLoginDetails = csv("data/loginDetails.csv").circular
val csvCustomerFeeder = csv("data/customer.csv").circular
object HomePage {
def mainPage = { exec(http("Load Home Page")
.get("/HomePage/") .resources(
http("Login Page") .get("/cgi-bin")
.check(regex("""value=\"(.*?)\"""").exists.saveAs("SessionId")), http("request_4")
.get("/HomePage/home.html"))) }
}
object Customer { def login = {
feed(csvFeederLoginDetails) .exec(http("Login Page")
.get("/cgi-bin") )
.exec(http("Customer Login Action") .post("/login.pl")
.formParam("userSession", "#{SessionId}") .formParam("username", "#{username}")
.formParam("password", "#{password}") )
) }
}
object Product {
def pay = { feed(csvCustomerFeeder)
http("Pay") .post("/cgi-bin/reserve")
.formParam("firstName", "#{firstName}") .formParam("lastName", "#{lastName}")
} }
val scn = scenario("WebToursTest2")
.exec(HomePage.mainPage)
.pause(2) .exec(Customer.login)
.pause(2) .exec(Product.pay)
